### Music Theory and Music Math

- `P.1`
  Equation:

### Color and Light

- `P.1`
  Equation:

  \[I_{\mathrm{P_1}}^+(\lambda) = \int K_{\mathrm{P_1}}(\lambda,\mu) I_{\mathrm{P_1}}^-(\mu)\, d\mu\]

  Variable legend: `I(lambda)` is spectral intensity; `K_line(lambda,mu)` is the transport kernel.
  Reading: structural fixation / extraction circuit / circulation circuit line.
  Confidence: mixed

### Game Theory

- `P.1`
  Equation:

  \[y_{\mathrm{P_1}}^+ = \operatorname*{argmin}_{y \in \Delta(\mathcal{A})}\{R_{\mathrm{P_1}}(y) + \lambda_{\mathrm{P_1}} C(y, y_{\mathrm{P_1}}^-)\}\]

  Variable legend: `y` is the strategy distribution; `R_line` is risk and `C` the control-cost.
  Reading: structural fixation / extraction circuit / circulation circuit line.
  Confidence: mixed
